\DoxyCodeLine{1190   \textcolor{comment}{// for inner local variables that do not represent functions won't}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1191   \textcolor{comment}{// result in any generated code.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1192   \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1193   \textcolor{comment}{// This will lead to multiple declaration nodes for the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1194   \textcolor{comment}{// same variable if it is declared several times. This is not a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1195   \textcolor{comment}{// semantic issue, but it may be a performance issue since it may}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1196   \textcolor{comment}{// lead to repeated DeclareEvalVar or DeclareEvalFunction calls.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1197   \mbox{\hyperlink{classv8_1_1internal_1_1Scope_a3fd4da9fa710b149c6d49ccb789cd396}{decls\_}}.Add(declaration);}
